      "source": [
        "data = pd.read_csv('covid-19-solution/data/data_start/_data_confirmed.csv')\n",
        "data_deaths = pd.read_csv('covid-19-solution/data/data_start/_data_deaths.csv')\n",
        "data_rus = pd.read_csv('covid-19-solution/data/data_start/_data_confirmed_rus.csv')\n",
        "data_deaths_rus = pd.read_csv('covid-19-solution/data/data_start/_data_deaths_rus.csv')"
      ],
      "execution_count": 0,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",

        "colab": {}
      },
      "source": [
        "cols1 = list(data.columns[:2]) + [i for i in data.columns[2:] if (pd.to_datetime(i) < pd.to_datetime(MIN_TEST))]\n",
        "data_train = data[cols1].append(data_rus[cols1])\n",
        "data_deaths_train = data_deaths[cols1].append(data_deaths_rus[cols1])\n",
        "\n",
        "cols2 = list(data.columns[:2]) + [i for i in data.columns[2:] if ((pd.to_datetime(i) >= pd.to_datetime(MIN_TEST)) & (pd.to_datetime(i) <= pd.to_datetime(MAX_TEST)))]\n",
        "data_test = data[cols2].append(data_rus[cols2])\n",
        "data_deaths_test = data_deaths[cols2].append(data_deaths_rus[cols2])"
      ],
      "execution_count": 0,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "ZNut_W7_Qg5n",
        "colab_type": "code",
        "colab": {}
      },
      "source": [
        "data_train2 = data_train.iloc[:,2:]\n",
        "data_train2v = np.log1p(data_train2.values)\n",
        "data_train2vt = (data_train2v - data_train2v.min()) / (data_train2v.max() - data_train2v.min())\n",
        "\n",
        "data_deaths_train2 = data_deaths_train.iloc[:,2:]\n",
        "data_deaths_train2v = np.log1p(data_deaths_train2.values)\n",
        "data_deaths_train2vt = (data_deaths_train2v - data_deaths_train2v.min()) / (data_deaths_train2v.max() - data_deaths_train2v.min())"
      ],
      "execution_count": 0,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "03NPAPUiQg7r",
        "colab_type": "code",
        "colab": {}
      },
      "source": [
        "model = Sequential()\n",
        "model.add(Dense(24, input_dim=data_train2vt.shape[1]))\n",
        "model.add(Dropout(0.02))\n",
        "model.add(Dense(data_train2vt.shape[1]))\n",
        "model.compile(loss='mean_squared_error', optimizer='adam')\n",
        "\n",
        "model_deaths = Sequential()\n",
        "model_deaths.add(Dense(24, input_dim=data_deaths_train2vt.shape[1]))\n",
        "model_deaths.add(Dropout(0.02))\n",
        "model_deaths.add(Dense(data_deaths_train2vt.shape[1]))\n",
        "model_deaths.compile(loss='mean_squared_error', optimizer='adam')"
      ],
      "execution_count": 0,
